<li id="cite_note-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-0">가</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-1">나</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-2">다</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-3">라</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-4">마</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand_4-5">바</a></sup></span> <span class="error mw-ext-cite-error" dir="ltr" lang="ko" xml:lang="ko">인용 오류: <code>&lt;ref&gt;</code> 태그가 잘못되었습니다; <code>RouteDecemberFourteenTwoThousand</code>라는 이름을 가진 주석에 제공한 텍스트가 없습니다</span></li>
